## intent:asking_someones_name
- what is your name?
- May I know your name?
- what is your name?
- wat is your name
- what is ur name?
- Tell me your name.
- What do I call you?
- what should I call you?
- what should I call u?
- what's your name?
- wat's ur name?
- What [could](grammar) be your name?
- tell me ur name.
